52 object arbitrary extends ArbitraryInstancesBinCompat0
53 
54 @deprecated(
55   "Use `arbitrary` instead. They were redundant, and that one is consistent with Cats.",
56   "0.22.6",
57 )
58 object ArbitraryInstances extends ArbitraryInstancesBinCompat0
59 
60 private[discipline] trait ArbitraryInstances { this: ArbitraryInstancesBinCompat0 =>
61 
62   implicit private class ParseResultSyntax[A](self: ParseResult[A]) {
63     def yolo: A = self.valueOr(e => sys.error(e.toString))
64   }
65 
66   implicit def http4sTestingArbitraryForNonEmptyList[A: Arbitrary]: Arbitrary[NonEmptyList[A]] =
67     Arbitrary {
68       for {
69         a <- getArbitrary[A]
70         list <- getArbitrary[List[A]]
71       } yield NonEmptyList(a, list)
72     }
73 
74   val genChar: Gen[Char] = choose('\u0000', '\u007F')
75 
76   val ctlChar: List[Char] = ('\u007F' +: ('\u0000' to '\u001F')).toList
77 
78   val lws: List[Char] = " \t".toList
79 
80   val genCrLf: Gen[String] = const("\r\n")
81 
82   val genRightLws: Gen[String] =
83     // No need to produce very long whitespaces
84     resize(5, nonEmptyListOf(oneOf(lws)).map(_.mkString))
85 
86   val genLws: Gen[String] =
87     oneOf(sequence[List[String], String](List(genCrLf, genRightLws)).map(_.mkString), genRightLws)
88 
89   val octets: List[Char] = ('\u0000' to '\u00FF').toList
90 
91   val genOctet: Gen[Char] = oneOf(octets)
92 
93   val allowedText: List[Char] = octets.diff(ctlChar)
94 
95   val genText: Gen[String] = oneOf(nonEmptyListOf(oneOf(allowedText)).map(_.mkString), genLws)
96 
97   // TODO Fix Rfc2616BasicRules.QuotedString to support the backslash character
98   val allowedQDText: List[Char] = allowedText.filterNot(c => c == '"' || c == '\\')
99 
100   val genQDText: Gen[String] = nonEmptyListOf(oneOf(allowedQDText)).map(_.mkString)
101 
102   @deprecated(
103     "Generates encoded values instead of the expected unencoded values that arbitraries should.  Use genQDText instead.",
104     "0.22.5",
105   )
106   val genQuotedPair: Gen[String] =
107     genChar.map(c => s"\\$c")
108 
109   @deprecated(
110     "Generates encoded values instead of the expected unencoded values that arbitraries should.  Use genQDText instead.",
111     "0.22.5",
112   )
113   val genQuotedString: Gen[String] = oneOf(genQDText, genQuotedPair).map(s => s"""\"$s\"""")
114 
115   private val tchars =
116     Set('!', '#', '$', '%', '&', '\'', '*', '+', '-', '.', '^', '_', '`', '|', '~') ++
117       ('0' to '9') ++ ('A' to 'Z') ++ ('a' to 'z')
118 
119   val genTchar: Gen[Char] = oneOf(tchars)
120 
121   val genToken: Gen[String] =
122     nonEmptyListOf(genTchar).map(_.mkString)
123 
124   val genNonTchar: Gen[Char] = frequency(
125     4 -> oneOf(Set(0x00.toChar to 0x7f.toChar: _*) -- tchars),
126     1 -> oneOf(0x100.toChar to Char.MaxValue),
127   )
128 
129   val genNonToken: Gen[String] = for {
130     a <- stringOf(genTchar)
131     b <- nonEmptyListOf(genNonTchar).map(_.mkString)
132     c <- stringOf(genChar)
133   } yield a + b + c
134 
135   val genVchar: Gen[Char] =
136     oneOf('\u0021' to '\u007e')
137 
138   val genFieldVchar: Gen[Char] =
139     genVchar
140 
141   val genFieldContent: Gen[String] =
142     for {
143       head <- genFieldVchar
144       tail <- containerOf[Vector, Vector[Char]](
145         frequency(
146           9 -> genFieldVchar.map(Vector(_)),
147           1 -> (for {
148             spaces <- nonEmptyContainerOf[Vector, Char](oneOf(' ', '\t'))
149             fieldVchar <- genFieldVchar
150           } yield spaces :+ fieldVchar),
151         )
152       ).map(_.flatten)
153     } yield (head +: tail).mkString
154 
155   val genFieldValue: Gen[String] =
156     genFieldContent
157 
158   val genStandardMethod: Gen[Method] =
159     oneOf(Method.all)
160 
161   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForMethod: Arbitrary[Method] = Arbitrary(
162     frequency(
163       10 -> genStandardMethod,
164       1 -> genToken.map(Method.fromString(_).yolo),
165     )
166   )
167   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForMethod: Cogen[Method] =
168     Cogen[Int].contramap(_.##)
169 
170   val genValidStatusCode: Gen[Int] =
171     choose(Status.MinCode, Status.MaxCode)
172 
173   val genStandardStatus: Gen[Status] =
174     oneOf(Status.registered)
175 
176   @deprecated(
177     "Custom status phrases will be removed in 1.0. They are an optional feature, pose a security risk, and already unsupported on some backends.",
178     "0.22.6",
179   )
180   val genCustomStatus: Gen[Status] = for {
181     code <- genValidStatusCode
182     reason <- genCustomStatusReason
183   } yield Status.fromInt(code).yolo.withReason(reason)
184 
185   @nowarn("cat=deprecation")
186   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForStatus: Arbitrary[Status] = Arbitrary(
187     frequency(
188       4 -> genStandardStatus,
189       1 -> genCustomStatus,
190     )
191   )
192   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForStatus: Cogen[Status] =
193     Cogen[Int].contramap(_.code)
194 
195   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForQueryParam: Arbitrary[(String, Option[String])] =
196     Arbitrary {
197       frequency(
198         5 -> {
199           for {
200             k <- getArbitrary[String]
201             v <- getArbitrary[Option[String]]
202           } yield (k, v)
203         },
204         2 -> const("foo" -> Some("bar")), // Want some repeats
205       )
206     }
207 
208   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForQuery: Arbitrary[Query] =
209     Arbitrary {
210       for {
211         n <- size
212         vs <- containerOfN[Vector, (String, Option[String])](
213           n % 8,
214           http4sTestingArbitraryForQueryParam.arbitrary,
215         )
216       } yield Query(vs: _*)
217     }
218 
219   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForHttpVersion: Arbitrary[HttpVersion] = {
220     val genSpecified = Gen.oneOf(HttpVersion.specified)
221     val genAll = for {
222       major <- Gen.chooseNum(0, 9)
223       minor <- Gen.chooseNum(0, 9)
224     } yield HttpVersion.fromVersion(major, minor).yolo
225     Arbitrary(Gen.oneOf(genSpecified, genAll))
226   }
227 
228   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForHttpVersion: Cogen[HttpVersion] =
229     Cogen[(Int, Int)].contramap(v => (v.major, v.minor))
230 
231   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForNioCharset: Arbitrary[NioCharset] =
232     Arbitrary(oneOf(Charset.availableCharsets))
233 
234   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForNioCharset: Cogen[NioCharset] =
235     Cogen[String].contramap(_.name)
236 
237   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForCharset: Arbitrary[Charset] =
238     Arbitrary(getArbitrary[NioCharset].map(Charset.fromNioCharset))
239 
240   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForCharset: Cogen[Charset] =
241     Cogen[NioCharset].contramap(_.nioCharset)
242 
243   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForQValue: Arbitrary[QValue] =
244     Arbitrary {
245       oneOf(const(0), const(1000), choose(0, 1000))
246         .map(QValue.fromThousandths(_).yolo)
247     }
248   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForQValue: Cogen[QValue] =
249     Cogen[Int].contramap(_.thousandths)
250 
251   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForCharsetRange: Arbitrary[CharsetRange] =
252     Arbitrary {
253       for {
254         charsetRange <- genCharsetRangeNoQuality
255         q <- getArbitrary[QValue]
256       } yield charsetRange.withQValue(q)
257     }
258 
259   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForCharsetRange: Cogen[CharsetRange] =
260     Cogen[Either[(Charset, QValue), QValue]].contramap {
261       case CharsetRange.Atom(charset, qValue) =>
262         Left((charset, qValue))
263       case CharsetRange.`*`(qValue) =>
264         Right(qValue)
265     }
266 
267   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForCharsetAtomRange: Arbitrary[CharsetRange.Atom] =
268     Arbitrary {
269       for {
270         charset <- getArbitrary[Charset]
271         q <- getArbitrary[QValue]
272       } yield charset.withQuality(q)
273     }
274 
275   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForCharsetSplatRange: Arbitrary[CharsetRange.`*`] =
276     Arbitrary(getArbitrary[QValue].map(CharsetRange.`*`.withQValue(_)))
277 
278   def genCharsetRangeNoQuality: Gen[CharsetRange] =
279     frequency(
280       3 -> getArbitrary[Charset].map(CharsetRange.fromCharset),
281       1 -> const(CharsetRange.`*`),
282     )
283 
284   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForAcceptCharset: Arbitrary[`Accept-Charset`] =
285     Arbitrary {
286       for {
287         // make a set first so we don't have contradictory q-values
288         charsetRanges <- nonEmptyContainerOf[Set, CharsetRange](genCharsetRangeNoQuality)
289           .map(_.toVector)
290         qValues <- containerOfN[Vector, QValue](
291           charsetRanges.size,
292           http4sTestingArbitraryForQValue.arbitrary,
293         )
294         charsetRangesWithQ = charsetRanges.zip(qValues).map { case (range, q) =>
295           range.withQValue(q)
296         }
297       } yield `Accept-Charset`(charsetRangesWithQ.head, charsetRangesWithQ.tail: _*)
298     }
299 
300   def genContentCodingNoQuality: Gen[ContentCoding] =
301     Gen.frequency(
302       (10, oneOf(ContentCoding.standard.values.toSeq)),
303       (2, genToken.map(ContentCoding.unsafeFromString)),
304     )
305 
306   implicit val http4sTrstingArbitraryForContentCoding: Arbitrary[ContentCoding] =
307     Arbitrary {
308       for {
309         cc <- genContentCodingNoQuality
310         q <- getArbitrary[QValue]
311       } yield cc.withQValue(q)
312     }
313 
314   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForContentCoding: Cogen[ContentCoding] =
315     Cogen[String].contramap(_.coding.map(_.toUpper.toLower))
316 
317   // MediaRange expects the quoted pair without quotes
318   val http4sGenUnquotedPair: Gen[String] = genQDText
319 
320   val http4sGenMediaRangeExtension: Gen[(String, String)] =
321     for {
322       token <- genToken
323       value <- oneOf(http4sGenUnquotedPair, genQDText)
324     } yield (token, value)
325 
326   val http4sGenMediaRangeExtensions: Gen[Map[String, String]] =
327     Gen.listOf(http4sGenMediaRangeExtension).map(_.toMap)
328 
329   val http4sGenMediaType: Gen[MediaType] = oneOf(MediaType.all.values.toSeq)
330   implicit val http4sArbitraryMediaType: Arbitrary[MediaType] = Arbitrary(http4sGenMediaType)
331 
332   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForMediaType: Cogen[MediaType] =
333     Cogen[(String, String, Map[String, String])].contramap(m =>
334       (m.mainType, m.subType, m.extensions)
335     )
336 
337   val http4sGenMediaRange: Gen[MediaRange] =
338     for {
339       `type` <- genToken.map(_.toLowerCase)
340       extensions <- http4sGenMediaRangeExtensions
341     } yield new MediaRange(`type`, extensions)
342 
343   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForMediaRange: Arbitrary[MediaRange] =
344     Arbitrary(http4sGenMediaRange)
345 
346   implicit val http4sTestingCogenForMediaRange: Cogen[MediaRange] =
347     Cogen[(String, String, Map[String, String])].contramap { m =>
348       val effectiveSubtype = m match {
349         case mt: MediaType => mt.subType
350         case _ => "*"
351       }
352       (m.mainType, effectiveSubtype, m.extensions)
353     }
354 
355   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForAcceptEncoding: Arbitrary[`Accept-Encoding`] =
356     Arbitrary {
357       for {
358         // make a set first so we don't have contradictory q-values
359         contentCodings <- nonEmptyContainerOf[Set, ContentCoding](genContentCodingNoQuality)
360           .map(_.toVector)
361         qValues <- containerOfN[Vector, QValue](
362           contentCodings.size,
363           http4sTestingArbitraryForQValue.arbitrary,
364         )
365         contentCodingsWithQ = contentCodings.zip(qValues).map { case (coding, q) =>
366           coding.withQValue(q)
367         }
368       } yield `Accept-Encoding`(NonEmptyList.fromListUnsafe(contentCodingsWithQ.toList))
369     }
370 
371   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForContentEncoding: Arbitrary[`Content-Encoding`] =
372     Arbitrary {
373       for {
374         contentCoding <- genContentCodingNoQuality
375       } yield `Content-Encoding`(contentCoding)
376     }

378   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForContentType: Arbitrary[`Content-Type`] =
379     Arbitrary {
380       for {
381         mediaType <- getArbitrary[MediaType]
382         charset <- getArbitrary[Charset]
383       } yield `Content-Type`(mediaType, charset)
384     }

386   def genLanguageTagNoQuality: Gen[LanguageTag] =
387     frequency(
388       3 -> (for {
389         primaryTag <- genAlphaToken
390         subTags <- frequency(4 -> Nil, 1 -> listOf(genAlphaToken))
391       } yield LanguageTag(primaryTag, subTags = subTags)),
392       1 -> const(LanguageTag.`*`),
393     )
394 
395   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForLanguageTag: Arbitrary[LanguageTag] =
396     Arbitrary {
397       for {
398         lt <- genLanguageTagNoQuality
399         q <- getArbitrary[QValue]
400       } yield lt.copy(q = q)
401     }
402 
403   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForAcceptLanguage: Arbitrary[`Accept-Language`] =
404     Arbitrary {
405       for {
406         // make a set first so we don't have contradictory q-values
407         languageTags <- nonEmptyContainerOf[Set, LanguageTag](genLanguageTagNoQuality)
408           .map(_.toVector)
409         qValues <-
410           containerOfN[Vector, QValue](languageTags.size, http4sTestingArbitraryForQValue.arbitrary)
411         tagsWithQ = languageTags.zip(qValues).map { case (tag, q) => tag.copy(q = q) }
412       } yield `Accept-Language`(tagsWithQ.head, tagsWithQ.tail: _*)
413     }

415   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForUrlForm: Arbitrary[UrlForm] = Arbitrary {
416     // new String("\ufffe".getBytes("UTF-16"), "UTF-16") != "\ufffe".
417     // Ain't nobody got time for that.
418     getArbitrary[Map[String, Chain[String]]]
419       .map(s =>
420         s.map { case (k, v) =>
421           k.replace('\ufffe', 'a') -> v.map(_.replace('\ufffe', 'a'))
422         }
423       )
424       .map(UrlForm.apply)
425   }

432     }

491   val genHttpDate: Gen[HttpDate] = {
492     val min = ZonedDateTime
493       .of(1900, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0, 0, ZoneId.of("UTC"))
494       .toInstant
495       .toEpochMilli / 1000
496     val max = ZonedDateTime
497       .of(9999, 12, 31, 23, 59, 59, 0, ZoneId.of("UTC"))
498       .toInstant
499       .toEpochMilli / 1000
500     choose[Long](min, max).map(HttpDate.unsafeFromEpochSecond)
501   }
502 
503   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForDateHeader: Arbitrary[headers.Date] =
504     Arbitrary {
505       for {
506         httpDate <- genHttpDate
507       } yield headers.Date(httpDate)
508     }
509 
510   val genHttpExpireDate: Gen[HttpDate] = {
511     // RFC 2616 says Expires should be between now and 1 year in the future, though other values are allowed
512     val min = ZonedDateTime.of(LocalDateTime.now, ZoneId.of("UTC")).toInstant.toEpochMilli / 1000
513     val max = ZonedDateTime
514       .of(LocalDateTime.now.plusYears(1), ZoneId.of("UTC"))
515       .toInstant
516       .toEpochMilli / 1000
517     choose[Long](min, max).map(HttpDate.unsafeFromEpochSecond)
518   }
519 
520   val genFiniteDuration: Gen[FiniteDuration] =
521     // Only consider positive durations
522     Gen.posNum[Long].map(_.seconds)
523 
524   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForExpiresHeader: Arbitrary[headers.Expires] =
525     Arbitrary {
526       for {
527         date <- genHttpExpireDate
528       } yield headers.Expires(date)
529     }

631   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForServerSentEvent: Arbitrary[ServerSentEvent] = {
632     import ServerSentEvent._
633     def singleLineString: Gen[String] =
634       getArbitrary[String].suchThat { s =>
635         !s.contains("\r") && !s.contains("\n")
636       }
637     Arbitrary(
638       for {
639         data <- frequency(
640           8 -> singleLineString.map(Some.apply),
641           1 -> None,
642         )
643         comment <- frequency(
644           1 -> singleLineString.map(Some.apply),
645           8 -> None,
646         )
647         event <- frequency(
648           4 -> None,
649           1 -> singleLineString.map(Some.apply),
650         )
651         id <- frequency(
652           8 -> None,
653           1 -> Some(EventId.reset),
654           1 -> singleLineString.suchThat(_.nonEmpty).map(id => Some(EventId(id))),
655         )
656         retry <- frequency(
657           4 -> None,
658           1 -> posNum[Long].map(Some.apply),
659         )
660       } yield ServerSentEvent(
661         data,
662         event,
663         id,
664         retry.map(FiniteDuration(_, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS)),
665         comment,
666       )
667     )
668   }

681   implicit private def http4sTestingSemigroupForGen[T: Semigroup]: Semigroup[Gen[T]] =
682     new Semigroup[Gen[T]] {
683       def combine(g1: Gen[T], g2: Gen[T]): Gen[T] = for {
684         t1 <- g1
685         t2 <- g2
686       } yield t1 |+| t2

779   implicit val http4sTestingAbitraryForPath: Arbitrary[Uri.Path] = Arbitrary {
780     val genSegmentNzNc =
781       nonEmptyListOf(oneOf(genUnreserved, genPctEncoded, genSubDelims, const("@"))).map(_.mkString)
782     val genPChar = oneOf(genUnreserved, genPctEncoded, genSubDelims, const(":"), const("@"))
783     val genSegmentNz = nonEmptyListOf(genPChar).map(_.mkString)
784     val genSegment = listOf(genPChar).map(_.mkString)
785     val genPathEmpty = const("")
786     val genPathAbEmpty = listOf(const("/") |+| genSegment).map(_.mkString)
787     val genPathRootless = genSegmentNz |+| genPathAbEmpty
788     val genPathNoScheme = genSegmentNzNc |+| genPathAbEmpty
789     val genPathAbsolute = const("/") |+| opt(genPathRootless)
790 
791     oneOf(genPathAbEmpty, genPathAbsolute, genPathNoScheme, genPathRootless, genPathEmpty).map(
792       Uri.Path.unsafeFromString
793     )
794   }

799   /** https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc3986 */
800   implicit val http4sTestingArbitraryForUri: Arbitrary[Uri] = Arbitrary {
801     val genPChar = oneOf(genUnreserved, genPctEncoded, genSubDelims, const(":"), const("@"))
802     val genScheme = oneOf(Uri.Scheme.http, Uri.Scheme.https)
803 
804     val genFragment: Gen[Uri.Fragment] =
805       listOf(oneOf(genPChar, const("/"), const("?"))).map(_.mkString)
806 
807     for {
808       scheme <- Gen.option(genScheme)
809       authority <- Gen.option(http4sTestingArbitraryForAuthority.arbitrary)
810       path <- http4sTestingAbitraryForPath.arbitrary
811       query <- http4sTestingArbitraryForQuery.arbitrary
812       fragment <- Gen.option(genFragment)
813     } yield Uri(scheme, authority, path, query, fragment)
814   }

816   /** Creates an `Gen[Url]` with checking that a URI is converting to String
817     * and back to URI safely.
818     * Use this Gen with cautions - it may lead to tests performance degradation.
819     */
820   def createGenUri: Gen[Uri] =
821     http4sTestingArbitraryForUri.arbitrary.filter { uri =>
822       // Uri.renderString encode special chars in the fragment
823       // and after converting the Uri to Json, the fragment will be encoded
824       val convertedBackToUriWithFragment =
825         (f: Uri.Fragment) => Uri.fromString(uri.withoutFragment.toString).map(_.withFragment(f))
826       val parsedUri =
827         uri.fragment.fold(Uri.fromString(uri.toString))(convertedBackToUriWithFragment)
828 
829       parsedUri == Right(uri)
830     }
